### `Library - Variable Storage` -- 327 call(s) in corpus

Library - Variable Storage" provides functions that pass values from test methods to page and message handler methods that are called out of context and cannot be called directly. This provides a flexible way to store values when running tests because you do not need to have specific global variables for each scenario.

Source: `BCApps\src\Tools\Test Framework\Test Libraries\Variable Storage\src\LibraryVariableStorage.Codeunit.al`

### `Library - Agent` -- 0 call(s) in corpus

Provides test helper functions for creating and managing agent tasks, messages, and user interventions. This library simplifies agent testing by providing convenient methods to create tasks, simulate user input, wait for task completion, and capture test output.

Source: `Internal\Apps\SystemApp\TestLibrary\Agent\src\LibraryAgent.Codeunit.al`

#### `ContinueTaskAndWait` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `ContinueTaskAndWait(var AgentTask: Record "Agent Task")`

Continues a paused task or the task that is waiting for user input. This convenience method creates a user intervention, marks output messages as sent, and waits for the task to complete.

**Parameters:**

- `AgentTask` -- The agent task to continue. Will be refreshed with updated state.

#### `ContinueTaskAndWait` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `ContinueTaskAndWait(var AgentTask: Record "Agent Task"; UserInput: Text)`

Continues a paused task or the task that is waiting for user input with custom user input. This convenience method creates a user intervention, marks output messages as sent, and waits for the task to complete.

**Parameters:**

- `AgentTask` -- The agent task to continue. Will be refreshed with updated state.
- `UserInput` -- The user input text to provide when continuing the task.

#### `CreateMessageAndWait` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `CreateMessageAndWait(var AgentTaskMessageBuilder: Codeunit "Agent Task Message Builder"; var AgentTask: Record "Agent Task")`

Creates a new message for an existing agent task. The method will start the task immediately and wait for the task to complete. The task status is set to Ready after the message is created.

**Parameters:**

- `AgentTaskMessageBuilder` -- The agent task message builder codeunit used to create the message details and the target agent task. Returns with updated status set to Ready.
- `AgentTask` -- The agent task record that the message is associated with.

#### `RunTurnAndWait` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `RunTurnAndWait(AgentUserSecurityId: Guid; var AgentTask: Record "Agent Task"; AgentTestResourceProvider: Interface IAgentTestResourceProvider)`

Provides input to the agent based on the current turn's query and waits for the task to complete. For task input queries (detected by 'title' element): creates a task with from, title, message, and attachments. For intervention queries (detected by 'intervention' element): responds with a suggestion code or free-text instruction. Throws an error if the query contains both 'title' and 'intervention', or neither. We recommend using this method instead of using the granular methods that are defined below.

**Parameters:**

- `AgentUserSecurityId` -- The security ID of the agent user to give the task to.
- `AgentTask` -- The agent task record. Task will be created for input queries; must be the existing task for interventions.
- `AgentTestResourceProvider` -- Interface for resolving attachment files from the consuming test app's resources.

#### `RunTurnAndWait` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `RunTurnAndWait(AgentUserSecurityId: Guid; var AgentTask: Record "Agent Task")`

Provides input to the agent based on the current turn's query and waits for the task to complete. Overload without attachment support — use when the query has no attachments. We recommend using this method instead of using the granular methods that are defined below.

**Parameters:**

- `AgentUserSecurityId` -- The security ID of the agent user to give the task to.
- `AgentTask` -- The agent task record. Task will be created for input queries; must be the existing task for interventions.

#### `SetAgentTaskTimeout` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `SetAgentTaskTimeout(NewTimeout: Duration)`

Sets the agent task timeout. This value will be used for waiting on all task related methods like <see cref="CreateTaskAndWait"/>, <see cref="ContinueTaskAndWait"/>, <see cref="WaitForTaskToComplete"/>, <see cref="CreateUserInterventionAndWait"/> and other similar methods.

**Parameters:**

- `NewTimeout` -- The new timeout duration to set for all agent task operations.

#### `StopAllTasks` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `StopAllTasks()`

Stops all tasks for all agents. Use this to clean up tasks during test teardown.

**Parameters:**

- `AgentUserSecurityId` -- The unique identifier of the agent whose tasks should be deactivated.

#### `ValidateInterventionRequest` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `ValidateInterventionRequest(AgentTask: Record "Agent Task"; ExpectedInterventionRequest: Codeunit "Test Input Json")`

Validates the current intervention request against expected data from the test input. Uses Assert to fail the test with a descriptive message if any check fails. Checks that the task requires intervention, the type matches, and expected suggestions are present.

**Parameters:**

- `AgentTask` -- The agent task to validate.
- `ExpectedInterventionRequest` -- The expected intervention request data from the YAML.

#### `WaitForTaskToComplete` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `WaitForTaskToComplete(var AgentTask: Record "Agent Task")`

Waits for an agent task to complete, blocking until the task finishes or the default timeout is reached. This method should be used for end to end testing scenarios where the functionality to create task is invoked via product, e.g. through an action.

**Parameters:**

- `AgentTask` -- The agent task to wait for. Will be refreshed with final state.

### `Library Assert` -- 0 call(s) in corpus

#### `AreEqual` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `AreEqual(ExpectedVariant: Variant; ActualVariant: Variant; Msg: Text)`

Tests whether the specified values are equal and throws an exception if the two values are not equal.

**Parameters:**

- `ExpectedVariant` -- The first value to compare. This is the value the tests expects.
- `ActualVariant` -- The second value to compare. This is the value produced by the code under test.
- `Msg` -- The message to include in the exception when actual is not equal to expected. The message is shown in test results.

#### `AreEqual` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `AreEqual(Expected: Dictionary of [Text, Text]; Actual: Dictionary of [Text, Text])`

Tests whether the specified dictionaries are equal and throws an exception if the two dictionaries are not equal.

**Parameters:**

- `Expected` -- The first dicitonary to compare.
- `Actual` -- The second dictionary to compare.

#### `AreEqualDateTime` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `AreEqualDateTime(Expected: DateTime; Actual: DateTime; Msg: Text)`

Tests whether the specified DateTime values are equal and throws an exception if the two DateTime values are not equal. This function uses the high precision format type 1

**Parameters:**

- `Expected` -- The first DateTime value to compare. This is the DateTime value the tests expects.
- `Actual` -- The second DateTime value to compare. This is the DateTime value produced by the code under test.
- `Msg` -- The message to include in the exception when actual is not equal to expected. The message is shown in test results.

#### `AreEqualDateTime` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `AreEqualDateTime(Expected: DateTime; Actual: DateTime; Delta: Duration; Msg: Text)`

Tests whether the specified DateTime values are nearly equal and throws an exception if the two DateTime values are not nearly equal.

**Parameters:**

- `Expected` -- The first DateTime value to compare. This is the DateTime value the tests expects.
- `Actual` -- The second DateTime value to compare. This is the DateTime value produced by the code under test.
- `Delta` -- The maximum difference between the two DateTime values.
- `Msg` -- The message to include in the exception when actual is not equal to expected. The message is shown in test results.

#### `AreNearlyEqual` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `AreNearlyEqual(Expected: Decimal; Actual: Decimal; Delta: Decimal; Msg: Text)`

Tests whether the specified decimals are equal and throws an exception if the they are not equal.

**Parameters:**

- `Expected` -- The first value to compare. This is the value the tests expects.
- `Actual` -- The second value to compare. This is the value produced by the code under test.
- `Delta` -- The required accuracy. An exception will be thrown only if actual is different than expected by more than delta.
- `Msg` -- The message to include in the exception when actual is different than expected by more than delta. The message is shown in test results.

#### `AreNotEqual` -- 0 call(s)

Signature: `AreNotEqual(ExpectedVariant: Variant; ActualVariant: Variant; Msg: Text)`

**Parameters:**

- `ExpectedVariant` -- The first value to compare. This is the value the test expects not to match actual.
- `ActualVariant` -- The second value to compare. This is the value produced by the code under test.
- `Msg` -- The message to include in the exception when actual is not equal to expected. The message is shown in test results.
